English

Aupamanyava says that one should purify the sacrificer at his vital breath with all bunches together, with the combined formulas, “May the lord of cognition purify thee, may the lord of speech purify thee, may god Savitс╣Ы purify thee with the strainer without a crevice, by means of the rays of the shining sun.”
